$(window).load(function() {
    
        if (!wb.settings.isMobileDevice && !wb.settings.disableBackground) {
            var $leftBg = $('.left-bg'),
                $body = $('.main-content'),
                leftBackground = '',
                rightBackground = '',
                backgroundColor = '';
            
            if (leftBackground)
                $leftBg.css('background', leftBackground);
            if (rightBackground)
                $body.css('background', rightBackground);
            if (backgroundColor)
                $leftBg.css('background-color', backgroundColor);
        }
    

    
        (function ($) {
            var container = $('#brandVote');
            var redesignCatalog = $.fn.wildCatalog("isRedesign");

            var brandId = container.data('brandId');
            var data = {
                redesign: redesignCatalog
            };
            var url = '/favoritebrands/getvotes/' + brandId;
            $.post(url, data, function (html) {
                container.html(html);
            });
        })(jQuery);
    

    
        (function ($) {
            var $container = $(".j-recent-goods-container");
            var action = loadVisitedGoods;
            
            onScroll($container, '.visited', action);

            function loadVisitedGoods(container) {
                //console.log('loadVisitedGoods');
                $.post("/visitedgoods", { count: container.attr("data-count") }, function (html) {
                    container.html(html);
                    wb.carousel.renderProductPrices(container);
                }, "html");
            }

            function onScroll(container, eventNameSpace, action) {
                var eventName = 'scroll' + eventNameSpace;
                $(window).on(eventName, function () {
                    if (!wb.utils.isElementInViewport(container, true))
                        return;

                    $(window).off(eventNameSpace);
                    action(container);
                }).trigger(eventName);
            }
        })(jQuery);
    

    
        (function ($) {
            var container = $('.j-wb-kids-container');
            //getArticlesAjax(container);
            bindScroll('wbkids', container, getArticlesAjax);

            function bindScroll(eventNamespace, container, action) {
                var eventName = 'scroll.' + eventNamespace;
                $(window).on(eventName, function () {
                    wb.utils.isElementInViewport(container, true) && $(window).off(eventName) && action(container);
                }).trigger(eventName);
            }
            
            function extractSubjectsXcatalog(query){
                if(!query)
                    return;
                const idx = query.indexOf("subject=");
                if(idx !== -1){
                    query = query.substring(idx+8);
                    const idxEnd = query.indexOf('&');
                    if(idxEnd !== -1){
                        query = query.substring(0, idxEnd);
                    }
                    return query.split(';').join(',');
                }                
            }

            function getArticlesAjax(container) {
                var subjects, baseApiUrl = "https://articles-api.wildberries.ru/api/v1", ajaxUrl, query;
                var brandId = container.attr('data-brand-id');
                var filterModelSubjects = extractSubjectsXcatalog($("[data-xcatalog-query]").attr('data-xcatalog-query'))
                    || $("[data-filter-subjects]").data('filter-subjects');
                //console.log('getArticlesAjax ', container, brandId, filterModelSubjects);
                if (brandId === undefined && (!filterModelSubjects || filterModelSubjects.length === 0))
                    return;

                if (brandId) {
                    //brandId = 4623;
                    ajaxUrl = baseApiUrl + "/brands/articles";
                    query = "ids=" + brandId;
                } else {
                    subjects = filterModelSubjects;
                    ajaxUrl = baseApiUrl + "/subjects/articles";
                    query = "ids=" + subjects;
                    //query = "ids=231,7,4180,3339";//9
                }

                $.ajax({
                    type: "GET",
                    xhrFields: {
                        withCredentials: false
                    },
                    url: ajaxUrl,
                    data: query,
                    processData: false,
                    success: function (result) {
                        var showOnly = 3;
                        if (result.length < showOnly)
                            return;

                        if (result.length > showOnly)
                            result = result.splice(0, showOnly);

                        $.templates("wbkids", $('#wb-kids-tmpl').html());
                        var html = $.render.wbkids(result);
                        //console.log(container);
                        $('ul', container).html(html);
                        $('.j-header', container).removeClass('hide');
                    }
                });
            }
        })(jQuery);
    

    
            (function () {
                $.when(wb.utils.script.require(wb.settings.scripts.tagline, true)).done(function (v1) {
                    wb.tagline.init();
                });
            }());
    

(function($){                                      
	                if (!$ || !wb || !wb.utils || !wb.utils.script || !wb.settings || !wb.settings.scripts)
		                return;
	                $.when(wb.utils.script.require(wb.settings.scripts.browser), wb.utils.script.require(wb.settings.scripts.externalStat)).then(function() {
	                    if (!wb.browser || !wb.browser.isBot()){
			                wb.externalStatInit({
				                eventsInfo: '{"counterData":[{"counterType":1,"eventNames":["viewList","setEmail"]}],"productIds":[8373865,3096452,3096465]}',
				                criteoUidCookieName: 'criteo_uid',
				                criteoMappingKey: '308',
				                processingUrl: '/stats/counters-processing',
				                redirectForCriteo: 'https%3A%2F%2Fwww.wildberries.ru%2Fstats%2Fcriteotrack%3Fuserid%3D%40USERID%40'
			                });
		                }
	                });
                })(jQuery);
});
</script>
